#  About this item 
  * REDESIGNED TO DO MORE: The redesigned Galaxy SmartTag2 is made so you can keep calm and keep track; Its design makes it easy for you to tag and carry your belongings 
  * EASY TO USE: It's IP67-rated water- and dust-resistant, activates your compatible IoT devices and stays powered for up to 500 days or even up to 40% more on Non-Power Saving Mode 
  * RELAX, YOU'VE GOT IT TAGGED: Simply register a new Galaxy SmartTag2 and get started right away with SmartThings Find; With its intuitive tracking experience, you now have a way to keep track of things you love right in the palm of your hand 
  * SEARCH NEAR WHEN IT'S NOT FAR: Lose something. Switch on Search Nearby and get guided instructions to your item's location via Compass View; If you still don't see it, just ring your Galaxy SmartTag2 to have it send out an audible signal 
  * Type of battery needed: replaceable CR2032 1 ea Lithium battery (not included)

##  Product Description 
The all-new Galaxy SmartTag2 is your ultimate tool for keeping track of the things that matter most¬π.  
  
¬πRequires Samsung Galaxy smartphones or tablets running Android 11.0 or later with 3GB or more of free RAM; user must opt-in to the SmartThings Find App and be logged in to Samsung Account. Bluetooth range of up to 120m without obstacles; if Galaxy SmartTag2 is out of range, Find Network will be used to track (Find Network accuracy based on opt-in Galaxy users who are in-range of the SmartTag). ¬≤Consistent with IP67 rating, water resistant in up to 1M (3 feet) of water for up to 30 minutes. Rinse residue / dry after wet. ¬≥Through the SmartThings app, allows 2 pre-set conditions at a time. A pre-set condition can be either an IoT device or a SmartThings routine. ‚Å¥Expected performance based on typical use with in-box CR2032 battery. Actual battery life may vary depending on different usage patterns, environmental conditions, the replacement battery manufacturer, and other factors. ‚ÅµNon-Power Saving Mode expected battery life under typical usage conditions is up to 500 days. Power Saving Mode is limited to basic Bluetooth finding functions (for example, Search Nearby signal indicator and map). ‚Å∂Requires Bluetooth, range up to 120m without obstacles; accuracy may be reduced if there's an obstacle between you and the tag, such as when the tag is inside a drawer, behind a wall, or in a car. Samsung account log-in and registration on SmartThings Find App is required. ‚Å∑Only available with ultra-wideband (UWB) enabled Galaxy smartphones running Android 11.0 or higher (Galaxy Note20 Ultra, S21+ and Ultra, S22+ and Ultra, S23+ and Ultra, Z Fold2 and up). Samsung account log-in and registration on SmartThings Find App is required. ‚Å∏Accessories sold separately. Color and availability may vary by carrier and retailer. ‚ÅπSamsung Galaxy smartphones and tablets sold separately.

[How customer reviews and ratings work](javascript:void\(0\))
Customer Reviews, including Product Star Ratings help customers to learn more about the product and decide whether it is the right product for them.
To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we don‚Äôt use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also analyzed reviews to verify trustworthiness.

### Customers say
Customers find the tracker easy to set up and appreciate its compatibility with Samsung Galaxy phones, though some report it won't pair with their devices. The tracking capability and ease of finding items receive mixed feedback - while some say it's great for tracking keys and luggage, others find it only shows general locations. The battery life and value for money also get mixed reviews, with some saying it's worth the money while others consider it a waste of money. The overall quality receives mixed opinions, with some describing it as a cool product while others find it terrible.

When the Mazda app subscription free trial expired, I needed something to track my vehicle where there wasn't a monthly service fee. In comes the Galaxy SmartTag2. I have a Galaxy phone so it was a no brainer. The tracking works as advertised and setting it up was seamlessly. When the device is near your phone or at least within the range of the bluetooth, it'll track the location almost exactly. But if it is out of the range of your phone, it'll ping nearby Galaxy phones to approximate its location which is usually accurate. Works best if the device is stationary.

##### [_5.0 out of 5 stars_ They work just as promised, and great price! ](https://www.amazon.com/gp/customer-reviews/R1YBBBWV5HKAXK/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)
Reviewed in the United States on May 19, 2025
Color: Black/White[Verified Purchase](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)
Great tags and work as promised! Very easy to set up. All I had to do was pull the blue tab out, a pairing request popped up on my phone and opened smartthings. It also notified of an update. You can change the ringtone and volume in the app as well. Its pretty loud, 105 db, which is about the decibels as many car alarms. However, its a tiny speaker, so don't expect it to sound as loud as a car alarm!  
  
As far as quality, of course, they're Samsung! Very durable and small enough to hide it in a purse, or even a wallet. If you're using for keys you won't need an additional key ring, it pretty much has one built into it. And its not bad looking either. You can get various protective covers for them as well. I highly recommend, especially at the current price reduction!  
  
Please know your tech products... I'm seeing bad reviews (not just for this item, but many) based on finding the tags when their phone isn't close enough to the tags. The location does not update until you are within the tags bluetooth range OR until another Samsung device grabs its location (meaning any other Samsung device belonging to anyone is near by, it automatically pings its location and then you immediately get the update).  
  
Furthermore, the reviews saying they went [x amount of feet (like 300) in the wrong direction] and its not picking up the tag, if you're retracing your footsteps for a lost item, you'll find it, so why would you go somewhere you were not to begin with? Illogical reasoning and illogical testing (also, what barriers could have been obstructing the signal, etc). And if an item was stolen, your hidden tag WILL ping once the signal is grabbed. Please stop giving bad reviews because you didn't research what you purchased and have no idea how it actually works.  
  
S/n: there are apps made by android developers that may bypass both the restriction to use these tags with other android phones, and the ability to find with locators other than via smartthings. However, I wouldn't base buying an item like this off of using a 3rd party app (especially if little is known about the app), and can also be removed at any moment.

##### [_5.0 out of 5 stars_ Worry no more! ](https://www.amazon.com/gp/customer-reviews/R1JACM6138FTQW/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)
Reviewed in the United States on September 15, 2024
Color: Black[Verified Purchase](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)
The Samsung Galaxy SmartTag2 is a modern tracking device designed to help you keep track of your belongings. Here‚Äôs a detailed review highlighting its features, benefits, and some potential drawbacks:  
  
Features:  
Bluetooth Tracking:  
  
Precision Tracking: The SmartTag2 uses Bluetooth technology to help you locate your items within a specified range. This range is typically up to 120 meters (about 394 feet) under ideal conditions.  
Find My Mobile Integration: It integrates with Samsung's Find My Mobile app, allowing for easy tracking and management of the tag.  
Design and Build:  
  
Compact and Durable: The SmartTag2 is small, lightweight, and designed to be durable. It can easily be attached to keyrings, bags, or other items.  
Design Options: It typically comes in various colors and styles, making it versatile and customizable to suit personal preferences.  
Battery Life:  
  
Long-Lasting Battery: The device often boasts an impressive battery life, lasting up to several months on a single charge, depending on usage and environmental conditions.  
Enhanced Features:  
  
UWB Technology: Some models incorporate Ultra-Wideband (UWB) technology for more precise location tracking. This feature can improve the accuracy of locating items within a close range.  
Smart Features: The tag can be used for various smart home integrations, such as controlling smart devices with customizable buttons.  
Sound Alerts:  
  
Audible Alerts: If you‚Äôre within range, you can make the SmartTag2 emit a sound to help you locate it more easily.  
Community Find:  
  
Galaxy Ecosystem: If the SmartTag2 is out of range, it can leverage the Galaxy network of devices to help locate it. This means other Samsung devices can anonymously report the location of your SmartTag2.  
Pros:  
Easy to Use: The setup process is straightforward, especially for users within the Samsung ecosystem. Integration with the Find My Mobile app is smooth and user-friendly.  
  
Effective Tracking: The device generally offers reliable tracking capabilities, with the UWB technology providing an extra layer of precision.  
  
Long Battery Life: The extended battery life reduces the frequency of recharges or battery changes.  
  
Durability: Its compact and durable design makes it suitable for everyday use and capable of withstanding some rough handling.  
  
Community Assistance: The ability to leverage the Galaxy ecosystem for tracking can be highly beneficial if your item is lost out of range.  
  
Cons:  
Compatibility: Primarily designed for Samsung devices, which means users with non-Samsung smartphones might experience limited functionality or integration issues.  
  
Range Limitation: While effective within its Bluetooth range, the SmartTag2 may not be as effective for locating items over longer distances.  
  
Price: Depending on the region and retailer, it might be slightly more expensive compared to other similar Bluetooth trackers on the market.  
  
Privacy Concerns: As with any tracking device, there could be privacy concerns about the tracking and sharing of location data, though Samsung implements various security measures.  
  
Summary:  
The Samsung Galaxy SmartTag2 is a versatile and effective tracking device, particularly well-suited for users within the Samsung ecosystem. Its combination of Bluetooth and UWB technologies, along with the long battery life and smart features, makes it a valuable tool for keeping track of personal belongings. While it is highly functional, its primary compatibility with Samsung devices and potential cost are considerations to keep in mind.
